```rust
                    self.parse_type()?
                };
                params.push((param_name, ty));
                if !self.eat(TokenKind::Comma).is_some() {
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        self.expect(TokenKind::RParen, "')'")?;

        let return_type = if self.check_keyword(&["返回", "return", "fanhui"]) {
            self.advance();
            self.parse_type()?
        } else {
            Type::Unit
        };

        let where_clause = if self.check_keyword(&["其中", "where"]) {
            self.parse_where_clause()?
        } else {
            Vec::new()
        };

        let mut preconditions = Vec::new();
        let mut postconditions = Vec::new();
        while self.check_keyword(&["前置", "requires"]) {
            self.advance();
            self.expect(TokenKind::Colon, "':'")?;
            preconditions.push(self.parse_expr()?);
        }
        while self.check_keyword(&["后置", "ensures"]) {
            self.advance();
            self.expect(TokenKind::Colon, "':'")?;
            postconditions.push(self.parse_expr()?);
        }

        // 函数体
        self.expect_keyword(&["开始", "begin"])?;  // 或直接 '{'
        let body = self.parse_block()?;
        let end_span = self.expect_keyword(&["结束", "end", "jieshu"])?.span;

        Ok(Item::Function(Function {
            public,
            name,
            generics,
            params,
            return_type,
            where_clause,
            preconditions,
            postconditions,
            body,
            span: start.merge(end_span),
        }))
    }

    fn parse_generic_params(&mut self) -> Result<Vec<GenericParam>, ParseError> {
        self.expect(TokenKind::Lt, "'<'")?;
        let mut params = Vec::new();
        loop {
            let name = self.parse_ident()?;
            let mut bounds = Vec::new();
            if self.eat(TokenKind::Colon).is_some() {
                loop {
                    bounds.push(self.parse_path()?);
                    if !self.eat(TokenKind::Plus).is_some() {
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            let default = if self.eat(TokenKind::Assign).is_some() {
                Some(self.parse_type()?)
            } else {
                None
            };
            params.push(GenericParam { name, bounds, default });
            if !self.eat(TokenKind::Comma).is_some() {
                break;
            }
        }
        self.expect(TokenKind::Gt, "'>'")?;
        Ok(params)
    }

    fn parse_where_clause(&mut self) -> Result<Vec<WherePredicate>, ParseError> {
        self.expect_keyword(&["其中", "where"])?;
        let mut preds = Vec::new();
        loop {
            let ty = self.parse_type()?;
            self.expect(TokenKind::Colon, "':'")?;
            let mut bounds = Vec::new();
            loop {
                bounds.push(self.parse_path()?);
                if !self.eat(TokenKind::Plus).is_some() {
                    break;
                }
            }
            preds.push(WherePredicate::TypeBound { ty, bounds });
            if !self.eat(TokenKind::Comma).is_some() {
                break;
            }
        }
        Ok(preds)
    }
}
```

### 4.8.2 结构体解析

```rust
impl Parser {
    fn parse_struct(&mut self, public: bool) -> Result<Item, ParseError> {
        let start = self.current_span();
        self.expect_keyword(&["结构", "struct", "jiegou"])?;
        let name = self.parse_ident()?;
        let generics = if self.check(TokenKind::Lt) {
            self.parse_generic_params()?
        } else {
            Vec::new()
        };
        let where_clause = if self.check_keyword(&["其中", "where"]) {
            self.parse_where_clause()?
        } else {
            Vec::new()
        };

        self.expect(TokenKind::LBrace, "'{'")?;
        let mut fields = Vec::new();
        while !self.check(TokenKind::RBrace) {
            self.expect_keyword(&["字段", "field", "ziduan"])?;
            let field_name = self.parse_ident()?;
            self.expect_keyword(&["类型", "type", "leixing"])?;
            let ty = self.parse_type()?;
            let default = if self.eat(TokenKind::Assign).is_some() {
                Some(self.parse_expr()?)
            } else {
                None
            };
            fields.push((field_name, ty, default));
            if !self.eat(TokenKind::Comma).is_some() && !self.check(TokenKind::RBrace) {
                // 允许换行分隔，不强制逗号
            }
        }
        let end_span = self.expect(TokenKind::RBrace, "'}'")?.span;

        Ok(Item::Struct(Struct {
            public,
            name,
            generics,
            where_clause,
            fields,
            span: start.merge(end_span),
        }))
    }
}
```

### 4.8.3 导入语句解析

```rust
impl Parser {
    fn parse_import(&mut self) -> Result<Item, ParseError> {
        let start = self.expect_keyword(&["导入", "import", "daoru"])?.span;
        let items = if self.check(TokenKind::LBrace) {
            self.advance();
            let mut idents = Vec::new();
            loop {
                idents.push(self.parse_ident()?);
                if !self.eat(TokenKind::Comma).is_some() {
                    break;
                }
            }
            self.expect(TokenKind::RBrace, "'}'")?;
            self.expect_keyword(&["从", "from", "cong"])?;
            Some(idents)
        } else {
            None
        };

        let path_tok = self.current().ok_or_else(|| ParseError::UnexpectedEof {
            expected: "模块路径".to_string(),
        })?;
        let path = match &path_tok.kind {
            TokenKind::StringLit(s) => s.clone(),
            TokenKind::Ident(s) => s.clone(),
            _ => return Err(ParseError::UnexpectedToken {
                expected: "字符串或标识符".to_string(),
                found: path_tok.clone(),
                span: path_tok.span,
            }),
        };
        self.advance();

        Ok(Item::Import(Import {
            items,
            path,
            span: start.merge(path_tok.span),
        }))
    }
}
```

### 4.8.4 外部块解析

```rust
impl Parser {
    fn parse_extern(&mut self) -> Result<Item, ParseError> {
        let start = self.expect_keyword(&["外部", "extern"])?.span;
        let abi = if self.check(TokenKind::StringLit("C".to_string())) {
            self.advance();
            ExternAbi::C
        } else {
            ExternAbi::C  // 默认
        };

        self.expect(TokenKind::LBrace, "'{'")?;
        let mut items = Vec::new();
        while !self.check(TokenKind::RBrace) {
            if self.check_keyword(&["函数", "func", "hanshu"]) {
                self.advance();
                let name = self.parse_ident()?;
                self.expect(TokenKind::LParen, "'('")?;
                let mut params = Vec::new();
                if !self.check(TokenKind::RParen) {
                    loop {
                        let param_name = self.parse_ident()?;
                        self.expect(TokenKind::Colon, "':'")?;
                        let ty = self.parse_type()?;
                        params.push((param_name, ty));
                        if !self.eat(TokenKind::Comma).is_some() {
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
                self.expect(TokenKind::RParen, "')'")?;
                let return_type = if self.check_keyword(&["返回", "return", "fanhui"]) {
                    self.advance();
                    self.parse_type()?
                } else {
                    Type::Unit
                };
                items.push(ExternItem::Function {
                    name,
                    generics: Vec::new(),
                    params,
                    return_type,
                    variadic: false,
                });
            } else if self.check_keyword(&["令", "let", "ling"]) || self.check_keyword(&["定", "const", "ding"]) {
                let mutable = self.check_keyword(&["令", "let", "ling"]);
                self.advance();
                let name = self.parse_ident()?;
                self.expect(TokenKind::Colon, "':'")?;
                let ty = self.parse_type()?;
                items.push(ExternItem::Static { name, ty, mutable });
            } else {
                let tok = self.current().unwrap().clone();
                return Err(ParseError::UnexpectedToken {
                    expected: "函数或变量声明".to_string(),
                    found: tok,
                    span: tok.span,
                });
            }
            self.eat(TokenKind::Semicolon);
        }
        let end_span = self.expect(TokenKind::RBrace, "'}'")?.span;

        Ok(Item::Extern(ExternBlock {
            abi,
            items,
            span: start.merge(end_span),
        }))
    }
}
```

## 4.9 错误恢复与报告

解析器在遇到语法错误时，会记录错误并尝试通过 `synchronize` 方法跳过部分 Token，以便继续解析后续内容，从而在一次编译中报告多个错误。

```rust
impl Parser {
    /// 解析顶层项，带错误恢复
    fn parse_item_with_recovery(&mut self) -> Option<Item> {
        match self.parse_item() {
            Ok(item) => Some(item),
            Err(e) => {
                self.errors.push(e);
                self.synchronize();
                None
            }
        }
    }

    /// 错误恢复：跳过若干 Token 直到遇到同步 Token
    fn synchronize(&mut self) {
        while !self.is_eof() {
            // 遇到这些 Token 时认为可以安全继续解析
            if self.check(TokenKind::Semicolon)
                || self.check(TokenKind::RBrace)
                || self.check_keyword(&["结束", "end", "jieshu"])
                || self.check_keyword(&["函数", "func", "hanshu"])
                || self.check_keyword(&["结构", "struct", "jiegou"])
                || self.check_keyword(&["模块", "module", "mokuai"])
            {
                self.advance(); // 消耗同步 Token
                return;
            }
            self.advance();
        }
    }
}
```

## 4.10 测试用例

```rust
#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    fn parse_source(source: &str) -> Program {
        let mut lexer = Lexer::new(source);
        let (tokens, _) = lexer.tokenize();
        let mut parser = Parser::new(tokens);
        parser.parse().unwrap()
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_parse_let() {
        let source = "令 年龄 为 25";
        let program = parse_source(source);
        assert_eq!(program.len(), 1);
        if let Item::Global(global) = &program[0] {
            assert_eq!(global.name.name, "年龄");
        } else {
            panic!("Expected global");
        }
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_parse_function() {
        let source = r#"
            函数 相加(甲 类型 整数, 乙 类型 整数) 返回 整数
            开始
                返回 甲 加 乙
            结束
        "#;
        let program = parse_source(source);
        assert_eq!(program.len(), 1);
        assert!(matches!(program[0], Item::Function(_)));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_parse_if() {
        let source = r#"
            若 年龄 大于 18 则
                显示("成年")
            否则
                显示("未成年")
            结束
        "#;
        let mut lexer = Lexer::new(source);
        let (tokens, _) = lexer.tokenize();
        let mut parser = Parser::new(tokens);
        let stmt = parser.parse_stmt().unwrap();
        assert!(matches!(stmt, Stmt::If { .. }));
    }
}
```

---

# 5. 抽象语法树（AST）完整定义

## 5.1 概述

抽象语法树（AST）是编译器前端输出的结构化中间表示，完整保留了源代码的语法结构和位置信息。幻语的 AST 设计遵循以下原则：

- **完整性**：每个语法结构都有对应的 AST 节点
- **位置追踪**：每个节点都携带源码范围（`SourceSpan`），便于错误报告和调试信息生成
- **可扩展性**：为未来的语言特性预留扩展空间
- **类型安全**：使用 Rust 的强类型系统表达各种语法变体

## 5.2 通用节点定义

### 5.2.1 源码位置与范围

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]
pub struct SourcePosition {
    /// 字节偏移（从文件开始，0-based）
    pub offset: usize,
    /// 行号（1-based）
    pub line: usize,
    /// 列号（按 UTF-8 字符计数，1-based）
    pub column: usize,
}

impl SourcePosition {
    pub const fn new(offset: usize, line: usize, column: usize) -> Self {
        Self { offset, line, column }
    }
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]
pub struct SourceSpan {
    pub start: SourcePosition,
    pub end: SourcePosition,
}

impl SourceSpan {
    pub fn new(start: SourcePosition, end: SourcePosition) -> Self {
        Self { start, end }
    }

    /// 合并两个 Span，返回覆盖两者的最小 Span
    pub fn merge(self, other: Self) -> Self {
        Self {
            start: self.start,
            end: other.end,
        }
    }

    /// 创建一个虚拟的默认 Span（用于测试或内部生成的节点）
    pub fn dummy() -> Self {
        Self {
            start: SourcePosition::new(0, 0, 0),
            end: SourcePosition::new(0, 0, 0),
        }
    }
}
```

### 5.2.2 标识符与路径

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]
pub struct Ident {
    pub name: String,
    pub span: SourceSpan,
}

impl Ident {
    pub fn new(name: String, span: SourceSpan) -> Self {
        Self { name, span }
    }

    pub fn dummy(name: &str) -> Self {
        Self {
            name: name.to_string(),
            span: SourceSpan::dummy(),
        }
    }
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub struct Path {
    pub segments: Vec<Ident>,
    pub generics: Option<Vec<Type>>,  // 路径上的泛型参数，如 Vec<i32>
    pub span: SourceSpan,
}

impl Path {
    /// 从单个标识符创建简单路径
    pub fn from_ident(ident: Ident) -> Self {
        Self {
            segments: vec![ident.clone()],
            generics: None,
            span: ident.span,
        }
    }
}
```

## 5.3 类型节点（Type）

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub enum Type {
    // === 基本数值类型 ===
    Int,       // 平台相关整数（64位）
    I8, I16, I32, I64,
    U8, U16, U32, U64,
    F32, F64,

    // === 其他基本类型 ===
    Bool,
    Char,
    String,
    Unit,      // 空类型，对应 ()

    // === 复合类型 ===
    List(Box<Type>),                           // 列表<T>
    Array(Box<Type>, Box<Expr>),               // 数组<T; N>
    Map(Box<Type>, Box<Type>),                 // 字典<K, V>
    Ptr(Box<Type>),                            // 指针<T>
    Option(Box<Type>),                         // 可选<T>

    // === 函数类型 ===
    Func(Vec<Type>, Box<Type>),                // (参数类型...) -> 返回类型

    // === 自定义类型 ===
    Named(Path),                               // 命名类型，如 模块::结构体

    // === 内部使用 ===
    Var(usize),                                // 类型推导变量（仅供类型推导器使用）
}

impl Type {
    /// 获取类型的源码范围（Named 类型可以从 Path 中获取，其他返回 dummy）
    pub fn span(&self) -> SourceSpan {
        match self {
            Type::Named(path) => path.span,
            _ => SourceSpan::dummy(),
        }
    }

    /// 判断是否为数值类型
    pub fn is_numeric(&self) -> bool {
        matches!(self,
            Type::Int | Type::I8 | Type::I16 | Type::I32 | Type::I64 |
            Type::U8 | Type::U16 | Type::U32 | Type::U64 |
            Type::F32 | Type::F64
        )
    }

    /// 判断是否为整数类型
    pub fn is_integer(&self) -> bool {
        matches!(self,
            Type::Int | Type::I8 | Type::I16 | Type::I32 | Type::I64 |
            Type::U8 | Type::U16 | Type::U32 | Type::U64
        )
    }
}
```

## 5.4 表达式节点（Expr）

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub enum Expr {
    // === 字面量 ===
    IntLit(i64, SourceSpan),
    FloatLit(f64, SourceSpan),
    StringLit(String, SourceSpan),
    CharLit(char, SourceSpan),
    BoolLit(bool, SourceSpan),
    Null(SourceSpan),

    // === 标识符 ===
    Ident(Ident),

    // === 二元运算 ===
    BinaryOp {
        op: BinaryOp,
        left: Box<Expr>,
        right: Box<Expr>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 一元运算 ===
    UnaryOp {
        op: UnaryOp,
        expr: Box<Expr>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 函数调用 ===
    Call {
        func: Box<Expr>,
        args: Vec<Expr>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 方法调用 ===
    MethodCall {
        receiver: Box<Expr>,
        method: Ident,
        args: Vec<Expr>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 字段访问 ===
    Field {
        target: Box<Expr>,
        field: Ident,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 索引访问 ===
    Index {
        target: Box<Expr>,
        index: Box<Expr>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 复合字面量 ===
    List(Vec<Expr>, SourceSpan),
    Map(Vec<(Expr, Expr)>, SourceSpan),
    Struct {
        path: Path,
        fields: Vec<(Ident, Expr)>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 闭包 ===
    Closure {
        params: Vec<(Ident, Option<Type>)>,
        return_type: Option<Type>,
        body: Vec<Stmt>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 条件表达式 ===
    IfExpr {
        cond: Box<Expr>,
        then_expr: Box<Expr>,
        else_expr: Box<Expr>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 模式匹配表达式 ===
    Match {
        expr: Box<Expr>,
        arms: Vec<(Pattern, Expr)>,
        default: Option<Box<Expr>>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 可选解包（? 运算符）===
    Try {
        expr: Box<Expr>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 类型断言 ===
    TypeAssertion {
        expr: Box<Expr>,
        ty: Type,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 内联汇编表达式 ===
    Asm(InlineAsm),
}

impl Expr {
    /// 获取表达式的源码范围
    pub fn span(&self) -> SourceSpan {
        match self {
            Expr::IntLit(_, span) => *span,
            Expr::FloatLit(_, span) => *span,
            Expr::StringLit(_, span) => *span,
            Expr::CharLit(_, span) => *span,
            Expr::BoolLit(_, span) => *span,
            Expr::Null(span) => *span,
            Expr::Ident(ident) => ident.span,
            Expr::BinaryOp { span, .. } => *span,
            Expr::UnaryOp { span, .. } => *span,
            Expr::Call { span, .. } => *span,
            Expr::MethodCall { span, .. } => *span,
            Expr::Field { span, .. } => *span,
            Expr::Index { span, .. } => *span,
            Expr::List(_, span) => *span,
            Expr::Map(_, span) => *span,
            Expr::Struct { span, .. } => *span,
            Expr::Closure { span, .. } => *span,
            Expr::IfExpr { span, .. } => *span,
            Expr::Match { span, .. } => *span,
            Expr::Try { span, .. } => *span,
            Expr::TypeAssertion { span, .. } => *span,
            Expr::Asm(asm) => asm.span,
        }
    }
}
```

### 5.4.1 运算符枚举

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]
pub enum BinaryOp {
    // 算术
    Add, Sub, Mul, Div, Mod,
    // 逻辑
    And, Or,
    // 比较
    Eq, Ne, Gt, Lt, Ge, Le,
    // 位运算
    Shl, Shr, BitAnd, BitOr, BitXor,
    // 赋值
    Assign,
    // 复合赋值
    AddAssign, SubAssign, MulAssign, DivAssign, ModAssign,
    ShlAssign, ShrAssign, BitAndAssign, BitOrAssign, BitXorAssign,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]
pub enum UnaryOp {
    Not,    // 逻辑非
    Neg,    // 负号
    BitNot, // 按位非
}
```

## 5.5 语句节点（Stmt）

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub enum Stmt {
    // === 变量声明 ===
    Let {
        name: Ident,
        ty: Option<Type>,
        value: Box<Expr>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 常量声明 ===
    Const {
        name: Ident,
        ty: Option<Type>,
        value: Box<Expr>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 赋值 ===
    Assign {
        target: Box<Expr>,
        value: Box<Expr>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 条件语句 ===
    If {
        cond: Box<Expr>,
        then_block: Vec<Stmt>,
        else_ifs: Vec<(Expr, Vec<Stmt>)>,
        else_block: Option<Vec<Stmt>>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 模式匹配语句 ===
    Match {
        expr: Box<Expr>,
        arms: Vec<(Pattern, Vec<Stmt>)>,
        default: Option<Vec<Stmt>>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 固定次数循环 ===
    Repeat {
        count: Box<Expr>,
        body: Vec<Stmt>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 条件循环 ===
    While {
        cond: Box<Expr>,
        body: Vec<Stmt>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 遍历循环 ===
    ForEach {
        var: Ident,
        iterable: Box<Expr>,
        body: Vec<Stmt>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    // === 返回语句 ===
    Return(Option<Box<Expr>>, SourceSpan),

    // === 控制流 ===
    Break(SourceSpan),
    Continue(SourceSpan),

    // === 内联汇编语句 ===
    Asm(InlineAsm, SourceSpan),

    // === 表达式语句 ===
    Expr(Box<Expr>, SourceSpan),
}

impl Stmt {
    pub fn span(&self) -> SourceSpan {
        match self {
            Stmt::Let { span, .. } => *span,
            Stmt::Const { span, .. } => *span,
            Stmt::Assign { span, .. } => *span,
            Stmt::If { span, .. } => *span,
            Stmt::Match { span, .. } => *span,
            Stmt::Repeat { span, .. } => *span,
            Stmt::While { span, .. } => *span,
            Stmt::ForEach { span, .. } => *span,
            Stmt::Return(_, span) => *span,
            Stmt::Break(span) => *span,
            Stmt::Continue(span) => *span,
            Stmt::Asm(_, span) => *span,
            Stmt::Expr(_, span) => *span,
        }
    }
}
```

## 5.6 模式匹配节点（Pattern）

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub enum Pattern {
    /// 通配符 `_`
    Wildcard(SourceSpan),

    /// 标识符绑定
    Ident(Ident),

    /// 字面量模式（如 `42`, `"hello"`, `true`）
    Literal(Expr),

    /// 结构体模式 `Point { x, y: 0 }`
    Struct {
        path: Path,
        fields: Vec<(Ident, Pattern)>,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },

    /// 列表模式 `[a, b, ..rest]`
    List(Vec<Pattern>, SourceSpan),

    /// 或模式 `A | B`
    Or(Box<Pattern>, Box<Pattern>, SourceSpan),
}

impl Pattern {
    pub fn span(&self) -> SourceSpan {
        match self {
            Pattern::Wildcard(span) => *span,
            Pattern::Ident(ident) => ident.span,
            Pattern::Literal(expr) => expr.span(),
            Pattern::Struct { span, .. } => *span,
            Pattern::List(_, span) => *span,
            Pattern::Or(_, _, span) => *span,
        }
    }
}
```

## 5.7 内联汇编节点（InlineAsm）

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub struct InlineAsm {
    /// 汇编模板字符串（可能多段，用于分隔操作数）
    pub templates: Vec<String>,

    /// 输出操作数
    pub outputs: Vec<AsmOperand>,

    /// 输入操作数
    pub inputs: Vec<AsmOperand>,

    /// 破坏列表（寄存器名或 "memory"、"cc"）
    pub clobbers: Vec<String>,

    /// 汇编选项
    pub options: AsmOptions,

    pub span: SourceSpan,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub struct AsmOperand {
    /// 可选的符号名（用于模板中按名称引用）
    pub name: Option<Ident>,

    /// 约束字符串（如 "r", "=r", "+r", "{rax}"）
    pub constraint: String,

    /// 操作数表达式
    pub expr: Expr,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default, PartialEq)]
pub struct AsmOptions {
    pub volatile: bool,        // 是否禁止优化重排
    pub pure: bool,            // 是否无副作用
    pub nomem: bool,           // 是否不读写内存
    pub preserves_flags: bool, // 是否保留条件码
    pub noreturn: bool,        // 是否不返回
    pub alignstack: bool,      // 是否需要栈对齐
    pub intel_syntax: bool,    // 是否使用 Intel 语法
}
```

## 5.8 顶层项节点（Item）

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub enum Item {
    Function(Function),
    Struct(Struct),
    Trait(Trait),
    Impl(Impl),
    Module(Module),
    Import(Import),
    Extern(ExternBlock),
    TypeAlias(TypeAlias),
    Global(Global),
}

impl Item {
    pub fn span(&self) -> SourceSpan {
        match self {
            Item::Function(f) => f.span,
            Item::Struct(s) => s.span,
            Item::Trait(t) => t.span,
            Item::Impl(i) => i.span,
            Item::Module(m) => m.span,
            Item::Import(i) => i.span,
            Item::Extern(e) => e.span,
            Item::TypeAlias(t) => t.span,
            Item::Global(g) => g.span,
        }
    }
}
```

### 5.8.1 函数（Function）

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub struct Function {
    /// 是否公开
    pub public: bool,

    /// 函数名
    pub name: Ident,

    /// 泛型参数
    pub generics: Vec<GenericParam>,

    /// 函数参数（名称，类型）
    pub params: Vec<(Ident, Type)>,

    /// 返回类型
    pub return_type: Type,

    /// where 子句约束
    pub where_clause: Vec<WherePredicate>,

    /// 前置条件（requires）
    pub preconditions: Vec<Expr>,

    /// 后置条件（ensures）
    pub postconditions: Vec<Expr>,

    /// 函数体
    pub body: Vec<Stmt>,

    /// 源码范围
    pub span: SourceSpan,
}
```

### 5.8.2 结构体（Struct）

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub struct Struct {
    pub public: bool,
    pub name: Ident,
    pub generics: Vec<GenericParam>,
    pub where_clause: Vec<WherePredicate>,
    /// 字段：(名称, 类型, 默认值)
    pub fields: Vec<(Ident, Type, Option<Expr>)>,
    pub span: SourceSpan,
}
```

### 5.8.3 特征（Trait）

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub struct Trait {
    pub public: bool,
    pub name: Ident,
    pub generics: Vec<GenericParam>,
    /// 父特征
    pub super_traits: Vec<Path>,
    /// 需要实现的方法签名
    pub methods: Vec<TraitMethod>,
    pub span: SourceSpan,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub struct TraitMethod {
    pub name: Ident,
    pub generics: Vec<GenericParam>,
    pub params: Vec<(Ident, Type)>,
    pub return_type: Type,
    pub where_clause: Vec<WherePredicate>,
    /// 是否有默认实现（在 trait 内部提供）
    pub default_body: Option<Vec<Stmt>>,
}
```

### 5.8.4 实现块（Impl）

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub struct Impl {
    pub generics: Vec<GenericParam>,
    /// 如果为 None，表示固有实现（impl Type）
    pub trait_name: Option<Path>,
    /// 目标类型
    pub target_type: Type,
    pub where_clause: Vec<WherePredicate>,
    pub methods: Vec<Function>,
    pub span: SourceSpan,
}
```

```rust
pub struct Module {

    pub items: Vec<Item>,
    pub span: SourceSpan,
}
```

### 5.8.6 导入（Import）

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub struct Import {
    /// 导入的具体项（None 表示导入整个模块）
    pub items: Option<Vec<Ident>>,
    /// 模块路径
    pub path: String,
    pub span: SourceSpan,
}
```

### 5.8.7 外部块（ExternBlock）

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub struct ExternBlock {
    pub abi: ExternAbi,
    pub items: Vec<ExternItem>,
    pub span: SourceSpan,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub enum ExternAbi {
    C,
    System,
    Rust,
    Custom(String),
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub enum ExternItem {
    Function {
        name: Ident,
        generics: Vec<GenericParam>,
        params: Vec<(Ident, Type)>,
        return_type: Type,
        variadic: bool,  // 是否可变参数（如 printf）
    },
    Static {
        name: Ident,
        ty: Type,
        mutable: bool,
    },
}
```

```rust
    pub name: Ident,
    pub generics: Vec<GenericParam>,
    pub ty: Type,
    pub span: SourceSpan,
}
```

### 5.8.9 全局变量/常量（Global）

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub struct Global {
    pub mutable: bool,  // true 表示变量（令），false 表示常量（定）
    pub name: Ident,
    pub ty: Option<Type>,
    pub value: Box<Expr>,
    pub span: SourceSpan,
}
```

## 5.9 泛型与约束

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub struct GenericParam {
    pub name: Ident,
    pub bounds: Vec<Path>,      // 类型约束（特征）
    pub default: Option<Type>,  // 默认类型
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub enum WherePredicate {
    /// 类型约束：T: Trait1 + Trait2
    TypeBound {
        ty: Type,
        bounds: Vec<Path>,
    },
    /// 生命周期约束：'a: 'b + 'c
    LifetimeBound {
        lifetime: Ident,
        bounds: Vec<Ident>,
    },
    /// 类型相等：T = U
    Equate {
        lhs: Type,
        rhs: Type,
    },
}
```

## 5.10 程序根节点

```rust
/// 整个程序的 AST 根节点
pub type Program = Vec<Item>;
```

## 5.11 AST 工具函数

```rust
/// AST 遍历器 trait
pub trait AstVisitor<T> {
    fn visit_item(&mut self, item: &Item) -> T;
    fn visit_stmt(&mut self, stmt: &Stmt) -> T;
    fn visit_expr(&mut self, expr: &Expr) -> T;
    fn visit_type(&mut self, ty: &Type) -> T;
    fn visit_pattern(&mut self, pattern: &Pattern) -> T;
}

/// AST 可变遍历器
pub trait AstVisitorMut {
    fn visit_item(&mut self, item: &mut Item);
    fn visit_stmt(&mut self, stmt: &mut Stmt);
    fn visit_expr(&mut self, expr: &mut Expr);
    fn visit_type(&mut self, ty: &mut Type);
    fn visit_pattern(&mut self, pattern: &mut Pattern);
}

/// 从 AST 中提取所有标识符（用于符号解析）
pub fn collect_idents(program: &Program) -> Vec<Ident> {
    struct IdentCollector(Vec<Ident>);
    impl AstVisitor<()> for IdentCollector {
        fn visit_expr(&mut self, expr: &Expr) {
            if let Expr::Ident(ident) = expr {
                self.0.push(ident.clone());
            }
        }
        fn visit_item(&mut self, _: &Item) {}
        fn visit_stmt(&mut self, _: &Stmt) {}
        fn visit_type(&mut self, _: &Type) {}
        fn visit_pattern(&mut self, pattern: &Pattern) {
            match pattern {
                Pattern::Ident(ident) => self.0.push(ident.clone()),
                Pattern::Struct { fields, .. } => {
                    for (_, p) in fields {
                        self.visit_pattern(p);
                    }
                }
                Pattern::List(patterns, _) => {
                    for p in patterns {
                        self.visit_pattern(p);
                    }
                }
                Pattern::Or(p1, p2, _) => {
                    self.visit_pattern(p1);
                    self.visit_pattern(p2);
                }
                _ => {}
            }
        }
    }
    let mut collector = IdentCollector(Vec::new());
    for item in program {
        collector.visit_item(item);
    }
    collector.0
}
```

## 5.12 完整示例：AST 构建

以下幻语源代码：

```hl
令 年龄 为 25
若 年龄 大于 18 则
    显示("成年")
结束
```

对应的 AST 结构示意（简化）：

```rust
Program(vec![
    Item::Global(Global {
        mutable: true,
        name: Ident::new("年龄".to_string(), span),
        ty: None,
        value: Box::new(Expr::IntLit(25, span)),
        span,
    }),
    // 注：语句不能直接放在顶层，实际会被包装在函数中
])
```

若包装在函数中：

```rust
Item::Function(Function {
    public: false,
    name: Ident::new("主".to_string(), span),
    generics: vec![],
    params: vec![],
    return_type: Type::Int,
    where_clause: vec![],
    preconditions: vec![],
    postconditions: vec![],
    body: vec![
        Stmt::Let {
            name: Ident::new("年龄".to_string(), span),
            ty: None,
            value: Box::new(Expr::IntLit(25, span)),
            span,
        },
        Stmt::If {
            cond: Box::new(Expr::BinaryOp {
                op: BinaryOp::Gt,
                left: Box::new(Expr::Ident(Ident::new("年龄".to_string(), span))),
                right: Box::new(Expr::IntLit(18, span)),
                span,
            }),
            then_block: vec![
                Stmt::Expr(
                    Box::new(Expr::Call {
                        func: Box::new(Expr::Ident(Ident::new("显示".to_string(), span))),
                        args: vec![Expr::StringLit("成年".to_string(), span)],
                        span,
                    }),
                    span,
                )
            ],
            else_ifs: vec![],
            else_block: None,
            span,
        }
    ],
    span,
})
```

---

# 6. 语义分析与类型系统

## 6.1 概述

语义分析阶段接收语法解析器输出的抽象语法树（AST），执行以下核心任务：

- **符号解析**：建立符号表，将标识符绑定到定义
- **类型检查与推导**：基于 Hindley-Milner 算法推导表达式类型，验证类型兼容性
- **所有权检查**（可选）：在所有权模式下，验证借用规则与生命周期
- **语义错误报告**：收集并报告类型不匹配、未定义变量、重复定义等错误

语义分析的结果是一个经过类型标注的 AST，以及一个可供后续编译阶段使用的符号表。

## 6.2 符号表（Symbol Table）

符号表管理程序中所有声明的符号（变量、函数、类型等），并维护作用域嵌套关系。

### 6.2.1 符号定义

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub struct Symbol {
    /// 符号名称
    pub name: String,
    /// 符号种类
    pub kind: SymbolKind,
    /// 符号类型（对于变量/函数）
    pub ty: Type,
    /// 是否可变（对于变量）
    pub mutable: bool,
    /// 可见性
    pub visibility: Visibility,
    /// 定义所在的源码范围
    pub span: SourceSpan,
    /// 定义所在的作用域深度（用于快速比较）
    pub scope_depth: usize,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
pub enum SymbolKind {
    Variable,       // 局部变量 / 全局变量
    Constant,       // 常量
    Function,       // 函数
    Struct,         // 结构体类型
    Trait,          // 特征
    Type,           // 类型别名
    Module,         // 模块
    GenericParam,   // 泛型参数
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
pub enum Visibility {
    Private,            // 模块内可见
    Public,             // 公开可见
    Exported(String),   // 导出为指定名称（用于 FFI）
}
```

### 6.2.2 作用域（Scope）

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct Scope {
    /// 本作用域内定义的符号（名称 → 符号）
    symbols: HashMap<String, Symbol>,
    /// 父作用域索引
    parent: Option<usize>,
    /// 作用域深度（0 为全局）
    depth: usize,
    /// 作用域对应的 AST 节点（用于错误报告）
    pub associated_node: ScopeNode,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]
pub enum ScopeNode {
    Module,
    Function,
    Block,
    Trait,
    Impl,
}

impl Scope {
    pub fn new(parent: Option<usize>, depth: usize, node: ScopeNode) -> Self {
        Self {
            symbols: HashMap::new(),
            parent,
            depth,
            associated_node: node,
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.2.3 符号表主结构

```rust
pub struct SymbolTable {
    /// 作用域栈，索引 0 为全局作用域
    scopes: Vec<Scope>,
    /// 当前作用域索引
    current_scope: usize,
    /// 模块路径（用于完全限定名）
    module_path: Vec<String>,
    /// 导入的符号映射（名称 → 完全限定名）
    imports: HashMap<String, String>,
}

impl SymbolTable {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        let global = Scope::new(None, 0, ScopeNode::Module);
        Self {
            scopes: vec![global],
            current_scope: 0,
            module_path: Vec::new(),
            imports: HashMap::new(),
        }
    }

    /// 进入新作用域
    pub fn enter_scope(&mut self, node: ScopeNode) {
        let depth = self.scopes[self.current_scope].depth + 1;
        let scope = Scope::new(Some(self.current_scope), depth, node);
        self.scopes.push(scope);
        self.current_scope = self.scopes.len() - 1;
    }

    /// 离开当前作用域
    pub fn exit_scope(&mut self) {
        if let Some(parent) = self.scopes[self.current_scope].parent {
            self.current_scope = parent;
        }
    }

    /// 在当前作用域定义符号
    pub fn define(
        &mut self,
        name: String,
        kind: SymbolKind,
        ty: Type,
        mutable: bool,
        visibility: Visibility,
        span: SourceSpan,
    ) -> Result<(), SemanticError> {
        let scope = &mut self.scopes[self.current_scope];
        if scope.symbols.contains_key(&name) {
            let existing = scope.symbols.get(&name).unwrap();
            return Err(SemanticError::DuplicateDefinition {
                name,
                first: existing.span,
                second: span,
            });
        }
        let depth = scope.depth;
        scope.symbols.insert(name.clone(), Symbol {
            name,
            kind,
            ty,
            mutable,
            visibility,
            span,
            scope_depth: depth,
        });
        Ok(())
    }

    /// 从当前作用域开始向外解析符号
    pub fn resolve(&self, name: &str) -> Option<&Symbol> {
        // 先检查导入
        if let Some(full_name) = self.imports.get(name) {
            // 简化：导入解析需要完全限定名查找
            // 实际实现需维护导入的符号映射
            return self.resolve_fully_qualified(full_name);
        }

        let mut scope_idx = self.current_scope;
        loop {
            let scope = &self.scopes[scope_idx];
            if let Some(sym) = scope.symbols.get(name) {
                return Some(sym);
            }
            if let Some(parent) = scope.parent {
                scope_idx = parent;
            } else {
                break;
            }
        }
        None
    }

    /// 可修改地解析符号
    pub fn resolve_mut(&mut self, name: &str) -> Option<&mut Symbol> {
        let mut scope_idx = self.current_scope;
        loop {
            let scope = &mut self.scopes[scope_idx];
            if scope.symbols.contains_key(name) {
                return scope.symbols.get_mut(name);
            }
            if let Some(parent) = scope.parent {
                scope_idx = parent;
            } else {
                break;
            }
        }
        None
    }

    /// 解析完全限定名（如 `模块::子模块::符号`）
    pub fn resolve_fully_qualified(&self, path: &str) -> Option<&Symbol> {
        // 实际实现需维护模块树
        None
    }

    /// 获取当前作用域深度
    pub fn current_depth(&self) -> usize {
        self.scopes[self.current_scope].depth
    }

    /// 获取所有作用域（用于调试）
    pub fn all_scopes(&self) -> &[Scope] {
        &self.scopes
    }
}
```

### 6.2.4 符号解析辅助方法

```rust
impl SymbolTable {
    /// 添加导入映射
    pub fn add_import(&mut self, alias: String, full_path: String) {
        self.imports.insert(alias, full_path);
    }

    /// 进入模块上下文
    pub fn enter_module(&mut self, name: String) {
        self.module_path.push(name);
        self.enter_scope(ScopeNode::Module);
    }

    /// 离开模块上下文
    pub fn exit_module(&mut self) {
        self.module_path.pop();
        self.exit_scope();
    }

    /// 获取当前模块的完全限定名前缀
    pub fn current_module_prefix(&self) -> String {
        self.module_path.join("::")
    }

    /// 检查名称是否为当前作用域的保留字（三语关键词已在词法层面处理）
    pub fn is_reserved(&self, name: &str) -> bool {
        // 关键词表已在词法分析器中定义，此处不需要重复检查
        false
    }
}
```

## 6.3 类型推导器（TypeInfer）

类型推导器基于 Hindley-Milner 算法，支持泛型、类型变量和 let 多态。

### 6.3.1 类型推导器结构

```rust
pub struct TypeInfer {
    /// 下一个可用的类型变量 ID
    next_var: usize,
    /// 类型变量替换表
    substitutions: HashMap<usize, Type>,
    /// 待合一的约束列表
    constraints: Vec<(Type, Type)>,
    /// 类型环境（变量名 → 类型）
    env: Vec<HashMap<String, Type>>,
    /// 符号表引用
    symbol_table: SymbolTable,
    /// 当前函数的返回类型（用于 return 语句检查）
    current_return_type: Option<Type>,
}

impl TypeInfer {
    pub fn new(symbol_table: SymbolTable) -> Self {
        Self {
            next_var: 0,
            substitutions: HashMap::new(),
            constraints: Vec::new(),
            env: vec![HashMap::new()],
            symbol_table,
            current_return_type: None,
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.3.2 类型变量管理

```rust
impl TypeInfer {
    /// 生成新的类型变量
    fn fresh_var(&mut self) -> Type {
        let var = self.next_var;
        self.next_var += 1;
        Type::Var(var)
    }

    /// 生成指定数量的新类型变量
    fn fresh_vars(&mut self, count: usize) -> Vec<Type> {
        (0..count).map(|_| self.fresh_var()).collect()
    }
}
```

### 6.3.3 合一（Unification）算法

```rust
impl TypeInfer {
    /// 对类型应用当前替换
    fn apply_subst(&self, ty: &Type) -> Type {
        match ty {
            Type::Var(v) => {
                if let Some(t) = self.substitutions.get(v) {
                    self.apply_subst(t)
                } else {
                    ty.clone()
                }
            }
            Type::List(inner) => Type::List(Box::new(self.apply_subst(inner))),
            Type::Array(inner, size) => Type::Array(Box::new(self.apply_subst(inner)), size.clone()),
            Type::Map(k, v) => Type::Map(
                Box::new(self.apply_subst(k)),
                Box::new(self.apply_subst(v)),
            ),
            Type::Ptr(inner) => Type::Ptr(Box::new(self.apply_subst(inner))),
            Type::Option(inner) => Type::Option(Box::new(self.apply_subst(inner))),
            Type::Func(params, ret) => Type::Func(
                params.iter().map(|t| self.apply_subst(t)).collect(),
                Box::new(self.apply_subst(ret)),
            ),
            _ => ty.clone(),
        }
    }

    /// 检查类型变量是否出现在某类型中（发生检查）
    fn occurs(&self, var: usize, ty: &Type) -> bool {
        match ty {
            Type::Var(v) => *v == var,
            Type::List(inner) => self.occurs(var, inner),
            Type::Array(inner, _) => self.occurs(var, inner),
            Type::Map(k, v) => self.occurs(var, k) || self.occurs(var, v),
            Type::Ptr(inner) => self.occurs(var, inner),
            Type::Option(inner) => self.occurs(var, inner),
            Type::Func(params, ret) => {
                params.iter().any(|t| self.occurs(var, t)) || self.occurs(var, ret)
            }
            _ => false,
        }
    }

    /// 合一两个类型
    fn unify(&mut self, t1: Type, t2: Type) -> Result<(), TypeError> {
        let t1 = self.apply_subst(&t1);
        let t2 = self.apply_subst(&t2);

        match (t1, t2) {
            (Type::Var(v1), Type::Var(v2)) if v1 == v2 => Ok(()),
            (Type::Var(v), t) => {
                if self.occurs(v, &t) {
                    Err(TypeError::Cyclic { span: SourceSpan::dummy() })
                } else {
                    self.substitutions.insert(v, t);
                    Ok(())
                }
            }
            (t, Type::Var(v)) => {
                if self.occurs(v, &t) {
                    Err(TypeError::Cyclic { span: SourceSpan::dummy() })
                } else {
                    self.substitutions.insert(v, t);
                    Ok(())
                }
            }
            (Type::Int, Type::Int) => Ok(()),
            (Type::I8, Type::I8) => Ok(()),
            (Type::I16, Type::I16) => Ok(()),
            (Type::I32, Type::I32) => Ok(()),
            (Type::I64, Type::I64) => Ok(()),
            (Type::U8, Type::U8) => Ok(()),
            (Type::U16, Type::U16) => Ok(()),
            (Type::U32, Type::U32) => Ok(()),
            (Type::U64, Type::U64) => Ok(()),
            (Type::F32, Type::F32) => Ok(()),
            (Type::F64, Type::F64) => Ok(()),
            (Type::Bool, Type::Bool) => Ok(()),
            (Type::Char, Type::Char) => Ok(()),
            (Type::String, Type::String) => Ok(()),
            (Type::Unit, Type::Unit) => Ok(()),

            (Type::List(a), Type::List(b)) => self.unify(*a, *b),
            (Type::Array(a, s1), Type::Array(b, s2)) => {
                // 大小也需要相等（常量求值后）
                self.unify(*a, *b)
            }
            (Type::Map(k1, v1), Type::Map(k2, v2)) => {
                self.unify(*k1, *k2)?;
                self.unify(*v1, *v2)
            }
            (Type::Ptr(a), Type::Ptr(b)) => self.unify(*a, *b),
            (Type::Option(a), Type::Option(b)) => self.unify(*a, *b),
            (Type::Func(p1, r1), Type::Func(p2, r2)) => {
                if p1.len() != p2.len() {
                    return Err(TypeError::Mismatch {
                        expected: Type::Func(p1, r1),
                        found: Type::Func(p2, r2),
                        span: SourceSpan::dummy(),
                    });
                }
                for (a, b) in p1.into_iter().zip(p2) {
                    self.unify(a, b)?;
                }
                self.unify(*r1, *r2)
            }
            (Type::Named(p1), Type::Named(p2)) if p1 == p2 => Ok(()),
            (a, b) => Err(TypeError::Mismatch {
                expected: a,
                found: b,
                span: SourceSpan::dummy(),
            }),
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.3.4 表达式类型推导

```rust
impl TypeInfer {
    /// 推导表达式的类型
    pub fn infer_expr(&mut self, expr: &Expr) -> Result<Type, TypeError> {
        let span = expr.span();
        match expr {
            Expr::IntLit(_, _) => Ok(Type::Int),
            Expr::FloatLit(_, _) => Ok(Type::F64),
            Expr::StringLit(_, _) => Ok(Type::String),
            Expr::CharLit(_, _) => Ok(Type::Char),
            Expr::BoolLit(_, _) => Ok(Type::Bool),
            Expr::Null(_) => Ok(self.fresh_var()), // 可赋值给任意可选类型

            Expr::Ident(ident) => {
                self.lookup_type(&ident.name)
                    .cloned()
                    .ok_or_else(|| TypeError::UnboundVariable {
                        name: ident.name.clone(),
                        span: ident.span,
                    })
            }

            Expr::BinaryOp { op, left, right, span } => {
                let t_left = self.infer_expr(left)?;
                let t_right = self.infer_expr(right)?;

                match op {
                    BinaryOp::Add | BinaryOp::Sub | BinaryOp::Mul | BinaryOp::Div | BinaryOp::Mod => {
                        // 算术运算要求左右类型一致
                        self.unify(t_left.clone(), t_right.clone())
                            .map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                        Ok(t_left)
                    }
                    BinaryOp::And | BinaryOp::Or => {
                        self.unify(t_left, Type::Bool).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                        self.unify(t_right, Type::Bool).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                        Ok(Type::Bool)
                    }
                    BinaryOp::Eq | BinaryOp::Ne | BinaryOp::Gt | BinaryOp::Lt
                    | BinaryOp::Ge | BinaryOp::Le => {
                        self.unify(t_left, t_right).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                        Ok(Type::Bool)
                    }
                    BinaryOp::Shl | BinaryOp::Shr | BinaryOp::BitAnd
                    | BinaryOp::BitOr | BinaryOp::BitXor => {
                        // 位运算要求整数类型
                        if !t_left.is_integer() || !t_right.is_integer() {
                            return Err(TypeError::InvalidOperation {
                                op: format!("{:?}", op),
                                left: t_left,
                                right: t_right,
                                span: *span,
                            });
                        }
                        self.unify(t_left.clone(), t_right).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                        Ok(t_left)
                    }
                    BinaryOp::Assign => {
                        self.unify(t_left, t_right).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                        Ok(Type::Unit)
                    }
                    _ => {
                        // 复合赋值等
                        self.unify(t_left.clone(), t_right).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                        Ok(Type::Unit)
                    }
                }
            }

            Expr::UnaryOp { op, expr, span } => {
                let t_expr = self.infer_expr(expr)?;
                match op {
                    UnaryOp::Not => {
                        self.unify(t_expr, Type::Bool).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                        Ok(Type::Bool)
                    }
                    UnaryOp::Neg => {
                        if !t_expr.is_numeric() {
                            return Err(TypeError::InvalidUnaryOperation {
                                op: "负号".to_string(),
                                ty: t_expr,
                                span: *span,
                            });
                        }
                        Ok(t_expr)
                    }
                    UnaryOp::BitNot => {
                        if !t_expr.is_integer() {
                            return Err(TypeError::InvalidUnaryOperation {
                                op: "按位非".to_string(),
                                ty: t_expr,
                                span: *span,
                            });
                        }
                        Ok(t_expr)
                    }
                }
            }

            Expr::Call { func, args, span } => {
                let t_func = self.infer_expr(func)?;
                match t_func {
                    Type::Func(param_tys, ret_ty) => {
                        if param_tys.len() != args.len() {
                            return Err(TypeError::ArgCountMismatch {
                                expected: param_tys.len(),
                                found: args.len(),
                                span: *span,
                            });
                        }
                        for (arg, expected) in args.iter().zip(param_tys.iter()) {
                            let t_arg = self.infer_expr(arg)?;
                            self.unify(t_arg, expected.clone()).map_err(|e| e.with_span(arg.span()))?;
                        }
                        Ok(*ret_ty)
                    }
                    _ => Err(TypeError::NotCallable {
                        ty: t_func,
                        span: func.span(),
                    }),
                }
            }

            Expr::MethodCall { receiver, method, args, span } => {
                // 方法调用需要查找 receiver 类型的方法表
                let t_receiver = self.infer_expr(receiver)?;
                self.resolve_method(&t_receiver, &method.name, args, *span)
            }

            Expr::Field { target, field, span } => {
                let t_target = self.infer_expr(target)?;
                self.resolve_field(&t_target, &field.name, *span)
            }

            Expr::Index { target, index, span } => {
                let t_target = self.infer_expr(target)?;
                let t_index = self.infer_expr(index)?;
                self.unify(t_index, Type::Int).map_err(|e| e.with_span(index.span()))?;

                match t_target {
                    Type::List(inner) => Ok(*inner),
                    Type::Array(inner, _) => Ok(*inner),
                    Type::Map(k, v) => {
                        // 索引类型需与键类型一致
                        self.unify(t_index, *k).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                        Ok(*v)
                    }
                    Type::String => Ok(Type::Char),
                    _ => Err(TypeError::NotIndexable {
                        ty: t_target,
                        span: *span,
                    }),
                }
            }

            Expr::List(elements, span) => {
                if elements.is_empty() {
                    Ok(Type::List(Box::new(self.fresh_var())))
                } else {
                    let mut elem_ty = self.infer_expr(&elements[0])?;
                    for elem in &elements[1..] {
                        let t = self.infer_expr(elem)?;
                        self.unify(elem_ty.clone(), t).map_err(|e| e.with_span(elem.span()))?;
                    }
                    Ok(Type::List(Box::new(elem_ty)))
                }
            }

            Expr::Map(pairs, span) => {
                if pairs.is_empty() {
                    Ok(Type::Map(Box::new(self.fresh_var()), Box::new(self.fresh_var())))
                } else {
                    let mut key_ty = self.infer_expr(&pairs[0].0)?;
                    let mut val_ty = self.infer_expr(&pairs[0].1)?;
                    for (k, v) in &pairs[1..] {
                        let tk = self.infer_expr(k)?;
                        let tv = self.infer_expr(v)?;
                        self.unify(key_ty.clone(), tk).map_err(|e| e.with_span(k.span()))?;
                        self.unify(val_ty.clone(), tv).map_err(|e| e.with_span(v.span()))?;
                    }
                    Ok(Type::Map(Box::new(key_ty), Box::new(val_ty)))
                }
            }

            Expr::Struct { path, fields, span } => {
                // 查找结构体定义，验证字段类型
                let struct_name = path.segments.last().unwrap().name.clone();
                let struct_def = self.symbol_table.resolve(&struct_name)
                    .ok_or_else(|| TypeError::UndefinedType {
                        name: struct_name,
                        span: path.span,
                    })?;

                // 实际实现需展开结构体定义，检查字段
                // 这里简化为返回命名类型
                Ok(Type::Named(path.clone()))
            }

            Expr::Closure { params, return_type, body, span } => {
                self.env.push(HashMap::new());
                let mut param_tys = Vec::new();
                for (name, anno) in params {
                    let ty = anno.clone().unwrap_or_else(|| self.fresh_var());
                    self.env.last_mut().unwrap().insert(name.name.clone(), ty.clone());
                    param_tys.push(ty);
                }

                let saved_return = self.current_return_type.clone();
                let ret_ty = return_type.clone().unwrap_or_else(|| self.fresh_var());
                self.current_return_type = Some(ret_ty.clone());

                for stmt in body {
                    self.infer_stmt(stmt)?;
                }

                self.current_return_type = saved_return;
                self.env.pop();

                Ok(Type::Func(param_tys, Box::new(ret_ty)))
            }

            Expr::IfExpr { cond, then_expr, else_expr, span } => {
                let t_cond = self.infer_expr(cond)?;
                self.unify(t_cond, Type::Bool).map_err(|e| e.with_span(cond.span()))?;

                let t_then = self.infer_expr(then_expr)?;
                let t_else = self.infer_expr(else_expr)?;

                self.unify(t_then.clone(), t_else).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                Ok(t_then)
            }

            Expr::Match { expr, arms, default, span } => {
                let t_expr = self.infer_expr(expr)?;
                let result_ty = self.fresh_var();

                for (pattern, arm_expr) in arms {
                    self.check_pattern(pattern, &t_expr)?;
                    self.env.push(HashMap::new());
                    self.bind_pattern(pattern, &t_expr)?;
                    let t_arm = self.infer_expr(arm_expr)?;
                    self.unify(result_ty.clone(), t_arm).map_err(|e| e.with_span(arm_expr.span()))?;
                    self.env.pop();
                }

                if let Some(default_expr) = default {
                    let t_default = self.infer_expr(default_expr)?;
                    self.unify(result_ty.clone(), t_default).map_err(|e| e.with_span(default_expr.span()))?;
                }

                Ok(result_ty)
            }

            Expr::Try { expr, span } => {
                let t_expr = self.infer_expr(expr)?;
                match t_expr {
                    Type::Option(inner) => Ok(*inner),
                    Type::Result(ok, _) => Ok(*ok),
                    _ => Err(TypeError::InvalidTry {
                        ty: t_expr,
                        span: *span,
                    }),
                }
            }

            Expr::TypeAssertion { expr, ty, span } => {
                let t_expr = self.infer_expr(expr)?;
                // 检查是否可以转换
                self.can_cast(&t_expr, ty).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                Ok(ty.clone())
            }

            Expr::Asm(asm) => {
                // 内联汇编的类型推导：根据输出约束推断
                self.infer_asm(asm)
            }
        }
    }

    /// 查找变量类型
    fn lookup_type(&self, name: &str) -> Option<&Type> {
        for scope in self.env.iter().rev() {
            if let Some(ty) = scope.get(name) {
                return Some(ty);
            }
        }
        None
    }

    /// 解析字段类型
    fn resolve_field(&mut self, ty: &Type, field: &str, span: SourceSpan) -> Result<Type, TypeError> {
        match ty {
            Type::Named(path) => {
                let struct_name = path.segments.last().unwrap().name.clone();
                // 查找结构体定义并返回字段类型
                // 实际实现需访问结构体定义表
                Err(TypeError::UndefinedField {
                    ty: ty.clone(),
                    field: field.to_string(),
                    span,
                })
            }
            _ => Err(TypeError::NoField {
                ty: ty.clone(),
                span,
            }),
        }
    }

    /// 解析方法调用类型
    fn resolve_method(&mut self, receiver: &Type, method: &str, args: &[Expr], span: SourceSpan) -> Result<Type, TypeError> {
        // 实际实现需查找方法表
        Err(TypeError::UndefinedMethod {
            ty: receiver.clone(),
            method: method.to_string(),
            span,
        })
    }

    /// 检查模式是否与类型匹配
    fn check_pattern(&mut self, pattern: &Pattern, ty: &Type) -> Result<(), TypeError> {
        match pattern {
            Pattern::Wildcard(_) => Ok(()),
            Pattern::Ident(_) => Ok(()),
            Pattern::Literal(lit) => {
                let t_lit = self.infer_expr(lit)?;
                self.unify(t_lit, ty.clone()).map_err(|e| e.with_span(pattern.span()))
            }
            Pattern::Struct { path, fields, span } => {
                // 检查结构体模式
                Ok(())
            }
            Pattern::List(patterns, span) => {
                match ty {
                    Type::List(inner) => {
                        for p in patterns {
                            self.check_pattern(p, inner)?;
                        }
                        Ok(())
                    }
                    _ => Err(TypeError::PatternMismatch {
                        pattern: format!("{:?}", pattern),
                        ty: ty.clone(),
                        span: *span,
                    }),
                }
            }
            Pattern::Or(p1, p2, span) => {
                self.check_pattern(p1, ty)?;
                self.check_pattern(p2, ty)
            }
        }
    }

    /// 将模式中的变量绑定到当前环境
    fn bind_pattern(&mut self, pattern: &Pattern, ty: &Type) -> Result<(), TypeError> {
        match pattern {
            Pattern::Ident(ident) => {
                self.env.last_mut().unwrap().insert(ident.name.clone(), ty.clone());
                Ok(())
            }
            Pattern::Struct { fields, .. } => {
                for (field, sub_pattern) in fields {
                    let field_ty = self.resolve_field(ty, &field.name, field.span)?;
                    self.bind_pattern(sub_pattern, &field_ty)?;
                }
                Ok(())
            }
            Pattern::List(patterns, _) => {
                match ty {
                    Type::List(inner) => {
                        for p in patterns {
                            self.bind_pattern(p, inner)?;
                        }
                        Ok(())
                    }
                    _ => Ok(()),
                }
            }
            _ => Ok(()),
        }
    }

    /// 检查类型转换是否合法
    fn can_cast(&self, from: &Type, to: &Type) -> Result<(), TypeError> {
        // 基本数值类型之间允许转换
        if from.is_numeric() && to.is_numeric() {
            return Ok(());
        }
        // 指针之间允许转换
        if matches!(from, Type::Ptr(_)) && matches!(to, Type::Ptr(_)) {
            return Ok(());
        }
        Err(TypeError::InvalidCast {
            from: from.clone(),
            to: to.clone(),
        })
    }

    /// 推导内联汇编的类型
    fn infer_asm(&mut self, asm: &InlineAsm) -> Result<Type, TypeError> {
        // 根据输出操作数推导
        if asm.outputs.is_empty() {
            Ok(Type::Unit)
        } else {
            // 简化：返回第一个输出操作数的类型
            self.infer_expr(&asm.outputs[0].expr)
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.3.5 语句类型检查

```rust
impl TypeInfer {
    /// 检查语句的类型正确性
    pub fn infer_stmt(&mut self, stmt: &Stmt) -> Result<(), TypeError> {
        match stmt {
            Stmt::Let { name, ty, value, span } => {
                let t_value = self.infer_expr(value)?;
                if let Some(anno) = ty {
                    self.unify(t_value.clone(), anno.clone()).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                }
                self.env.last_mut().unwrap().insert(name.name.clone(), ty.clone().unwrap_or(t_value));
                Ok(())
            }

            Stmt::Const { name, ty, value, span } => {
                let t_value = self.infer_expr(value)?;
                if let Some(anno) = ty {
                    self.unify(t_value.clone(), anno.clone()).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                }
                self.env.last_mut().unwrap().insert(name.name.clone(), ty.clone().unwrap_or(t_value));
                Ok(())
            }

            Stmt::Assign { target, value, span } => {
                let t_target = self.infer_expr(target)?;
                let t_value = self.infer_expr(value)?;
                self.unify(t_target, t_value).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))
            }

            Stmt::If { cond, then_block, else_ifs, else_block, span } => {
                let t_cond = self.infer_expr(cond)?;
                self.unify(t_cond, Type::Bool).map_err(|e| e.with_span(cond.span()))?;

                self.env.push(HashMap::new());
                for s in then_block { self.infer_stmt(s)?; }
                self.env.pop();

                for (cond, block) in else_ifs {
                    let t_cond = self.infer_expr(cond)?;
                    self.unify(t_cond, Type::Bool).map_err(|e| e.with_span(cond.span()))?;
                    self.env.push(HashMap::new());
                    for s in block { self.infer_stmt(s)?; }
                    self.env.pop();
                }

                if let Some(block) = else_block {
                    self.env.push(HashMap::new());
                    for s in block { self.infer_stmt(s)?; }
                    self.env.pop();
                }
                Ok(())
            }

            Stmt::Match { expr, arms, default, span } => {
                let t_expr = self.infer_expr(expr)?;

                for (pattern, block) in arms {
                    self.check_pattern(pattern, &t_expr)?;
                    self.env.push(HashMap::new());
                    self.bind_pattern(pattern, &t_expr)?;
                    for s in block { self.infer_stmt(s)?; }
                    self.env.pop();
                }

                if let Some(block) = default {
                    self.env.push(HashMap::new());
                    for s in block { self.infer_stmt(s)?; }
                    self.env.pop();
                }
                Ok(())
            }

            Stmt::Repeat { count, body, span } => {
                let t_count = self.infer_expr(count)?;
                self.unify(t_count, Type::Int).map_err(|e| e.with_span(count.span()))?;

                self.env.push(HashMap::new());
                for s in body { self.infer_stmt(s)?; }
                self.env.pop();
                Ok(())
            }

            Stmt::While { cond, body, span } => {
                let t_cond = self.infer_expr(cond)?;
                self.unify(t_cond, Type::Bool).map_err(|e| e.with_span(cond.span()))?;

                self.env.push(HashMap::new());
                for s in body { self.infer_stmt(s)?; }
                self.env.pop();
                Ok(())
            }

            Stmt::ForEach { var, iterable, body, span } => {
                let t_iter = self.infer_expr(iterable)?;
                let elem_ty = match t_iter {
                    Type::List(inner) => *inner,
                    Type::Array(inner, _) => *inner,
                    Type::String => Type::Char,
                    _ => return Err(TypeError::NotIterable {
                        ty: t_iter,
                        span: iterable.span(),
                    }),
                };

                self.env.push(HashMap::new());
                self.env.last_mut().unwrap().insert(var.name.clone(), elem_ty);
                for s in body { self.infer_stmt(s)?; }
                self.env.pop();
                Ok(())
            }

            Stmt::Return(expr, span) => {
                if let Some(expected) = &self.current_return_type {
                    if let Some(expr) = expr {
                        let t_expr = self.infer_expr(expr)?;
                        self.unify(t_expr, expected.clone()).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                    } else {
                        self.unify(Type::Unit, expected.clone()).map_err(|e| e.with_span(*span))?;
                    }
                } else {
                    return Err(TypeError::ReturnOutsideFunction { span: *span });
                }
                Ok(())
            }

            Stmt::Break(_) | Stmt::Continue(_) => {
                // 需在循环上下文中检查
                Ok(())
            }

            Stmt::Asm(asm, span) => {
                self.infer_asm(asm)?;
                Ok(())
            }

            Stmt::Expr(expr, _) => {
                self.infer_expr(expr)?;
                Ok(())
            }
        }
    }
}
```

### 6.3.6 顶层项类型检查

```rust
impl TypeInfer {
    /// 检查整个程序
    pub fn infer_program(&mut self, program: &Program) -> Result<(), Vec<TypeError>> {
        let mut errors = Vec::new();

        // 第一遍：收集所有顶层定义到符号表
        for item in program {
            if let Err(e) = self.collect_top_level(item) {
                errors.push(e);
            }
        }

        // 第二遍：类型检查每个项
        for item in program {
            if let Err(e) = self.check_item(item) {
                errors.push(e);
            }
        }

        if errors.is_empty() {
            Ok(())
        } else {
            Err(errors)
        }
    }

    fn collect_top_level(&mut self, item: &Item) -> Result<(), TypeError> {
        match item {
            Item::Function(func) => {
                let ty = Type::Func(
                    func.params.iter().map(|(_, t)| t.clone()).collect(),
                    Box::new(func.return_type.clone()),
                );
                self.symbol_table.define(
                    func.name.name.clone(),
                    SymbolKind::Function,
                    ty,
                    false,
                    if func.public { Visibility::Public } else { Visibility::Private },
                    func.span,
                ).map_err(|e| TypeError::SemanticError(e))
            }
            Item::Struct(s) => {
                self.symbol_table.define(
                    s.name.name.clone(),
                    SymbolKind::Struct,
                    Type::Unit, // 占位
                    false,
                    if s.public { Visibility::Public } else { Visibility::Private },
                    s.span,
                ).map_err(|e| TypeError::SemanticError(e))
            }
            Item::Global(g) => {
                self.symbol_table.define(
                    g.name.name.clone(),
                    if g.mutable { SymbolKind::Variable } else { SymbolKind::Constant },
                    g.ty.clone().unwrap_or(Type::Var(self.next_var)),
                    g.mutable,
                    Visibility::Private,
                    g.span,
                ).map_err(|e| TypeError::SemanticError(e))
            }
            // 其他项类似处理
            _ => Ok(()),
        }
    }

    fn check_item(&mut self, item: &Item) -> Result<(), TypeError> {
        match item {
            Item::Function(func) => self.check_function(func),
            Item::Struct(s) => self.check_struct(s),
            Item::Impl(imp) => self.check_impl(imp),
            Item::Global(g) => {
                let t_value = self.infer_expr(&g.value)?;
                if let Some(anno) = &g.ty {
                    self.unify(t_value, anno.clone()).map_err(|e| e.with_span(g.span))?;
                }
                Ok(())
            }
            _ => Ok(()),
        }
    }

    fn check_function(&mut self, func: &Function) -> Result<(), TypeError> {
        self.env.push(HashMap::new());
        self.current_return_type = Some(func.return_type.clone());

        for (name, ty) in &func.params {
            self.env.last_mut().unwrap().insert(name.name.clone(), ty.clone());
        }

        for stmt in &func.body {
            self.infer_stmt(stmt)?;
        }

        // 检查函数体是否以 return 或隐式返回结尾
        // （具体规则：最后一条语句若不是 return，且返回类型非 Unit，则报错）

        self.env.pop();
        self.current_return_type = None;
        Ok(())
    }

    fn check_struct(&mut self, s: &Struct) -> Result<(), TypeError> {
        for (_, ty, _) in &s.fields {
            // 验证字段类型是否已定义
            self.validate_type(ty)?;
        }
        Ok(())
    }

    fn check_impl(&mut self, imp: &Impl) -> Result<(), TypeError> {
        for method in &imp.methods {
            self.check_function(method)?;
        }
        Ok(())
    }

    fn validate_type(&self, ty: &Type) -> Result<(), TypeError> {
        match ty {
            Type::Named(path) => {
                let name = path.segments.last().unwrap().name.clone();
                if self.symbol_table.resolve(&name).is_none() {
                    return Err(TypeError::UndefinedType {
                        name,
                        span: path.span,
                    });
                }
                Ok(())
            }
            Type::List(inner) => self.validate_type(inner),
            Type::Array(inner, _) => self.validate_type(inner),
            Type::Map(k, v) => {
                self.validate_type(k)?;
                self.validate_type(v)
            }
            Type::Ptr(inner) => self.validate_type(inner),
            Type::Option(inner) => self.validate_type(inner),
            Type::Func(params, ret) => {
                for p in params { self.validate_type(p)?; }
                self.validate_type(ret)
            }
            _ => Ok(()),
        }
    }
}
```

## 6.4 语义错误类型

```rust
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub enum SemanticError {
    TypeError(TypeError),
    DuplicateDefinition {
        name: String,
        first: SourceSpan,
        second: SourceSpan,
    },
    InvalidAssignment {
        target: String,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    BreakOutsideLoop(SourceSpan),
    ContinueOutsideLoop(SourceSpan),
    ReturnOutsideFunction {
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub enum TypeError {
    Mismatch {
        expected: Type,
        found: Type,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    UnboundVariable {
        name: String,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    UndefinedType {
        name: String,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    UndefinedField {
        ty: Type,
        field: String,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    UndefinedMethod {
        ty: Type,
        method: String,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    Cyclic {
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    NotCallable {
        ty: Type,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    ArgCountMismatch {
        expected: usize,
        found: usize,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    InvalidOperation {
        op: String,
        left: Type,
        right: Type,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    InvalidUnaryOperation {
        op: String,
        ty: Type,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    NotIndexable {
        ty: Type,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    NotIterable {
        ty: Type,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    InvalidTry {
        ty: Type,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    InvalidCast {
        from: Type,
        to: Type,
    },
    PatternMismatch {
        pattern: String,
        ty: Type,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    NoField {
        ty: Type,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    SemanticError(SemanticError),
}

impl TypeError {
    pub fn with_span(self, span: SourceSpan) -> Self {
        match self {
            TypeError::Mismatch { expected, found, .. } => TypeError::Mismatch { expected, found, span },
            TypeError::UnboundVariable { name, .. } => TypeError::UnboundVariable { name, span },
            TypeError::Cyclic { .. } => TypeError::Cyclic { span },
            // 其他变体类似
            _ => self,
        }
    }
}
```

## 6.5 所有权检查器（可选）

所有权检查器在启用所有权模式时运行，验证借用规则。

```rust
pub struct BorrowChecker {
    /// 当前活跃的借用（内存位置 → 借用状态）
    loans: HashMap<MemoryLocation, Loan>,
    /// 符号表（用于获取变量信息）
    symbol_table: SymbolTable,
    /// 当前作用域深度
    scope_depth: usize,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]
struct MemoryLocation {
    var_id: usize,  // 变量的唯一标识
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
enum Loan {
    Shared(usize),  // 共享借用计数
    Mutable,        // 可变借用（只能有一个）
}

impl BorrowChecker {
    pub fn new(symbol_table: SymbolTable) -> Self {
        Self {
            loans: HashMap::new(),
            symbol_table,
            scope_depth: 0,
        }
    }

    pub fn check_function(&mut self, func: &Function) -> Result<(), BorrowError> {
        self.scope_depth = 0;
        for stmt in &func.body {
            self.check_stmt(stmt)?;
        }
        Ok(())
    }

    fn check_stmt(&mut self, stmt: &Stmt) -> Result<(), BorrowError> {
        match stmt {
            Stmt::Let { name, value, span, .. } => {
                self.check_expr(value)?;
                // 记录新变量
                Ok(())
            }
            Stmt::Assign { target, value, span } => {
                self.check_expr(target)?;
                self.check_expr(value)?;
                Ok(())
            }
            Stmt::Expr(expr, _) => {
                self.check_expr(expr)?;
                Ok(())
            }
            // 其他语句递归检查
            _ => Ok(()),
        }
    }

    fn check_expr(&mut self, expr: &Expr) -> Result<(), BorrowError> {
        match expr {
            Expr::Ident(ident) => {
                // 检查变量是否可读
                if let Some(sym) = self.symbol_table.resolve(&ident.name) {
                    if !sym.mutable {
                        // 不可变变量，无需借用检查
                        return Ok(());
                    }
                    // 检查当前借用状态
                    let loc = MemoryLocation { var_id: 0 }; // 实际需获取变量 ID
                    if let Some(Loan::Mutable) = self.loans.get(&loc) {
                        return Err(BorrowError::CannotBorrowWhileMutable {
                            name: ident.name.clone(),
                            span: ident.span,
                        });
                    }
                }
                Ok(())
            }
            Expr::BinaryOp { op, left, right, .. } => {
                self.check_expr(left)?;
                self.check_expr(right)?;
                Ok(())
            }
            Expr::Call { func, args, .. } => {
                self.check_expr(func)?;
                for arg in args {
                    self.check_expr(arg)?;
                }
                Ok(())
            }
            Expr::MethodCall { receiver, args, .. } => {
                self.check_expr(receiver)?;
                for arg in args {
                    self.check_expr(arg)?;
                }
                Ok(())
            }
            Expr::Field { target, .. } => {
                self.check_expr(target)?;
                Ok(())
            }
            // 其他表达式递归检查
            _ => Ok(()),
        }
    }
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
pub enum BorrowError {
    UseAfterMove {
        name: String,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    CannotBorrowWhileMutable {
        name: String,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    CannotBorrowMutableWhileShared {
        name: String,
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
    LifetimeMismatch {
        span: SourceSpan,
    },
}
```

## 6.6 语义分析驱动

```rust
pub struct SemanticAnalyzer {
    symbol_table: SymbolTable,
    type_infer: TypeInfer,
    borrow_checker: Option<BorrowChecker>,
    errors: Vec<SemanticError>,
}

impl SemanticAnalyzer {
    pub fn new(enable_ownership: bool) -> Self {
        let symbol_table = SymbolTable::new();
        let type_infer = TypeInfer::new(symbol_table.clone());
        let borrow_checker = if enable_ownership {
            Some(BorrowChecker::new(symbol_table.clone()))
        } else {
            None
        };
        Self {
            symbol_table,
            type_infer,
            borrow_checker,
            errors: Vec::new(),
        }
    }

    pub fn analyze(&mut self, program: &Program) -> Result<SymbolTable, Vec<SemanticError>> {
        // 类型检查
        if let Err(errs) = self.type_infer.infer_program(program) {
            self.errors.extend(errs.into_iter().map(|e| SemanticError::TypeError(e)));
        }

        // 所有权检查（如果启用）
        if let Some(checker) = &mut self.borrow_checker {
            for item in program {
                if let Item::Function(func) = item {
                    if let Err(e) = checker.check_function(func) {
                        self.errors.push(SemanticError::BorrowError(e));
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        if self.errors.is_empty() {
            Ok(self.symbol_table.clone())
        } else {
            Err(std::mem::take(&mut self.errors))
        }
    }
}
```

## 6.7 测试用例

```rust
#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn test_type_infer_simple() {
        let source = "令 年龄 为 25";
        let program = parse_source(source);
        let mut analyzer = SemanticAnalyzer::new(false);
        let result = analyzer.analyze(&program);
        assert!(result.is_ok());
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_type_mismatch() {
        let source = r#"
            函数 主() 返回 整数
            开始
                令 年龄 为 "二十五"
                返回 年龄
            结束
        "#;
        let program = parse_source(source);
        let mut analyzer = SemanticAnalyzer::new(false);
        let result = analyzer.analyze(&program);
        assert!(result.is_err());
    }
}
```

---

# 7. 内存管理与所有权模型

## 7.1 内存管理概述

幻语采用**无垃圾回收（No-GC）**的内存管理策略，提供两种可选的内存安全模式：

| 模式 | 触发方式 | 内存安全保证 | 运行时开销 |
|------|---------|-------------|-----------|
| **默认模式** | 默认（无特殊标志） | 编译期无检查，依赖开发者显式管理；调试构建提供边界检查 | 零额外开销 |
| **所有权模式** | `使用 所有权` 或 `--所有权` | 编译期借用检查，保证无悬垂指针、无数据竞争 | 零额外开销（编译期检查） |

两种模式均**禁止隐式堆分配**，所有动态内存分配必须通过分配器显式完成。这一设计使幻语能够胜任从裸机嵌入式到高性能服务器的全场景内存管理需求。

## 7.2 分配器接口（Allocator）

### 7.2.1 分配器特征定义

```rust
/// 分配器特征，所有堆内存操作必须通过实现了此特征的分配器进行
pub trait Allocator {
    /// 分配至少 `size` 字节、对齐为 `align` 的内存块
    /// 
    /// # 安全性
    /// - 返回的指针必须满足对齐要求
    /// - 若分配失败，返回 `std::ptr::null_mut()`
    fn alloc(&self, size: usize, align: usize) -> *mut u8;

    /// 释放之前由 `alloc` 分配的 `size` 字节、对齐为 `align` 的内存块
    /// 
    /// # 安全性
    /// - `ptr` 必须由同一分配器的 `alloc` 返回
    /// - `size` 和 `align` 必须与分配时一致
    fn free(&self, ptr: *mut u8, size: usize, align: usize);

    /// 重新分配内存块，将原有 `old_size` 字节的数据复制到新块，并释放旧块
    /// 
    /// # 安全性
    /// - `ptr` 必须由同一分配器的 `alloc` 或 `realloc` 返回
    /// - 若返回 `null`，则原有内存块保持不变
    fn realloc(&self, ptr: *mut u8, old_size: usize, new_size: usize, align: usize) -> *mut u8;
}
```

### 7.2.2 全局默认分配器

```rust
/// 全局默认分配器（使用系统 malloc/free）
pub struct GlobalAllocator;

impl Allocator for GlobalAllocator {
    fn alloc(&self, size: usize, align: usize) -> *mut u8 {
        // 在有操作系统环境下调用 libc::malloc 或 std::alloc::alloc
        #[cfg(feature = "std")]
        {
            let layout = std::alloc::Layout::from_size_align(size, align).unwrap();
            std::alloc::alloc(layout)
        }
        #[cfg(not(feature = "std"))]
        {
            // 裸机环境下需链接自定义的 malloc 实现
            extern "C" { fn malloc(size: usize) -> *mut u8; }
            unsafe { malloc(size) }
        }
    }

    fn free(&self, ptr: *mut u8, size: usize, align: usize) {
        #[cfg(feature = "std")]
        {
            let layout = std::alloc::Layout::from_size_align(size, align).unwrap();
            std::alloc::dealloc(ptr, layout);
        }
        #[cfg(not(feature = "std"))]
        {
            extern "C" { fn free(ptr: *mut u8); }
            unsafe { free(ptr); }
        }
    }

    fn realloc(&self, ptr: *mut u8, old_size: usize, new_size: usize, align: usize) -> *mut u8 {
        #[cfg(feature = "std")]
        {
            let layout = std::alloc::Layout::from_size_align(old_size, align).unwrap();
            std::alloc::realloc(ptr, layout, new_size)
        }
        #[cfg(not(feature = "std"))]
        {
            extern "C" { fn realloc(ptr: *mut u8, size: usize) -> *mut u8; }
            unsafe { realloc(ptr, new_size) }
        }
    }
}

/// 获取全局默认分配器的单例
pub fn default_allocator() -> &'static dyn Allocator {
    static GLOBAL: GlobalAllocator = GlobalAllocator;
    &GLOBAL
}
```

### 7.2.3 嵌入式分配器示例（首次适应）

```rust
/// 简单的首次适应分配器，适用于裸机嵌入式系统
pub struct FirstFitAllocator {
    /// 堆起始地址
    heap_start: usize,
    /// 堆总大小
    heap_size: usize,
    /// 空闲链表头指针
    free_list: *mut FreeBlock,
}

struct FreeBlock {
    size: usize,
    next: *mut FreeBlock,
}

impl FirstFitAllocator {
    /// 使用指定的静态内存区域初始化分配器
    pub const fn new(heap_start: usize, heap_size: usize) -> Self {
        Self {
            heap_start,
            heap_size,
            free_list: core::ptr::null_mut(),
        }
    }

    /// 初始化空闲链表（需在运行时调用一次）
    pub unsafe fn init(&mut self) {
        let block = self.heap_start as *mut FreeBlock;
        (*block).size = self.heap_size;
        (*block).next = core::ptr::null_mut();
        self.free_list = block;
    }
}

impl Allocator for FirstFitAllocator {
    fn alloc(&self, size: usize, align: usize) -> *mut u8 {
        // 遍历空闲链表，找到第一个足够大的块
        let mut current = self.free_list;
        let mut prev: *mut FreeBlock = core::ptr::null_mut();

        while !current.is_null() {
            let block = unsafe { &mut *current };
            let block_addr = current as usize;
            let aligned_addr = (block_addr + align - 1) & !(align - 1);
```
